<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="30" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="1376" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:2003" class="extiw" title="commons:Category:2003"><span style="">2003</span></a></b></i>.</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><b>2003</b> (<a href="/wiki/Roman_numerals" title="Roman numerals">MMIII</a>) was a <a href="/wiki/Common_year" title="Common year">common year</a> <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Wednesday" title="Common year starting on Wednesday">starting on Wednesday</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 2003rd year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 3rd  year of the <a href="/wiki/3rd_millennium" title="3rd millennium">3rd&#160;millennium</a>, the 3rd  year of the <a href="/wiki/21st_century" title="21st century">21st&#160;century</a>, and the  4th   year of the <a href="/wiki/2000s_(decade)" title="2000s (decade)">2000s</a> decade. </p><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">2003</div> 
<p>2003 was designated the International Year of <a href="/wiki/Fresh_water" title="Fresh water">Fresh water</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/January_11" title="January 11">January 11</a> – Illinois Governor <a href="/wiki/George_Ryan" title="George Ryan">George Ryan</a> commutes the death sentences of 167 prisoners on Illinois's death row based on the <a href="/wiki/Jon_Burge" title="Jon Burge">Jon Burge</a> scandal.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_22" title="January 22">January 22</a> – The last signal from NASA's <i><a href="/wiki/Pioneer_10" title="Pioneer 10">Pioneer 10</a></i> spacecraft is received, some 12.2 billion kilometers (7.6 billion mi) from <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">Earth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_30" title="January 30">January 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> <a href="/wiki/Same-sex_marriage_in_Belgium" title="Same-sex marriage in Belgium">legally recognizes same-sex marriage</a>, becoming the second country in the world to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/February_1" title="February 1">February 1</a> – At the conclusion of the <a href="/wiki/STS-107" title="STS-107">STS-107</a> mission, the <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia_disaster" title="Space Shuttle Columbia disaster">Space Shuttle <i>Columbia</i> disintegrates during reentry</a> over <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, killing all seven astronauts on board.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_4" title="February 4">February 4</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Serbia_and_Montenegro" title="Serbia and Montenegro">Federal Republic of Yugoslavia</a> is renamed to "Serbia and Montenegro" (after its constituent states) after its leaders reconstitute the country into a loose state-union between <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Montenegro_(1992%E2%80%932006)" title="Republic of Montenegro (1992–2006)">Montenegro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Serbia_(1992%E2%80%932006)" title="Republic of Serbia (1992–2006)">Serbia</a>, marking an end to the 73-year-long use of the name "Yugoslavia" by any sovereign state.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_15" title="February 15">February 15</a>–<a href="/wiki/February_16" title="February 16">16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Antwerp_diamond_heist" title="Antwerp diamond heist">Antwerp diamond heist</a>: An Italian gang steals loose diamonds, gold and jewellery valued at more than $100 million from a Belgian vault, one of the largest robberies in history.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_15" title="February 15">February 15</a> – Millions of people worldwide take part in massive <a href="/wiki/February_15,_2003,_anti-war_protests" class="mw-redirect" title="February 15, 2003, anti-war protests">anti-war protests</a> in anticipation of the United States and its allies invading <a href="/wiki/Ba%27athist_Iraq" title="Ba&#39;athist Iraq">Iraq</a> to depose its Ba'athist regime.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_18" title="February 18">February 18</a> – An arsonist <a href="/wiki/Daegu_subway_fire" title="Daegu subway fire">sets fire to a subway train</a> in Daegu, South Korea, killing 192 people.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_20" title="February 20">February 20</a> - <a href="/wiki/The_Station_nightclub_fire" title="The Station nightclub fire">The Station nightclub fire</a> occurs in <a href="/wiki/West_Warwick,_Rhode_Island" title="West Warwick, Rhode Island">West Warwick, Rhode Island</a>, killing 100 people and injuring 230 and another 132 escape uninjured.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_26" title="February 26">February 26</a> – The <a href="/wiki/War_in_Darfur" title="War in Darfur">War in Darfur</a> begins after rebel groups rise up against the Sudanese government.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_27" title="February 27">February 27</a> – Former Bosnian Serb leader <a href="/wiki/Biljana_Plav%C5%A1i%C4%87" title="Biljana Plavšić">Biljana Plavšić</a> is sentenced by the United Nations <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Tribunal_for_the_former_Yugoslavia" title="International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia">International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia</a> to 11 years in prison for war crimes committed during the <a href="/wiki/Bosnian_War" title="Bosnian War">Bosnian War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/March_8" title="March 8">March 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a> approves joining the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> in <a href="/wiki/2003_Maltese_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Maltese European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_12" title="March 12">March 12</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Serbia_(1992%E2%80%932006)" title="Republic of Serbia (1992–2006)">Serbian</a> Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Zoran_%C4%90in%C4%91i%C4%87" title="Zoran Đinđić">Zoran Đinđić</a> <a href="/wiki/Assassination_of_Zoran_%C4%90in%C4%91i%C4%87" title="Assassination of Zoran Đinđić">is assassinated in Belgrade</a> by a sniper.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> issues a global alert on <a href="/wiki/Severe_acute_respiratory_syndrome" title="Severe acute respiratory syndrome">severe acute respiratory syndrome</a> when it spreads to <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> after originating in <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_20" title="March 20">March 20</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Iraq_War" title="Iraq War">Iraq War</a> begins with the <a href="/wiki/2003_invasion_of_Iraq" title="2003 invasion of Iraq">invasion</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ba%27athist_Iraq" title="Ba&#39;athist Iraq">Iraq</a> by the U.S. and allied forces.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_23" title="March 23">March 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Slovenia" title="Slovenia">Slovenia</a> approves joining the European Union and <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> in <a href="/wiki/2003_Slovenian_European_Union_and_NATO_membership_referendum" title="2003 Slovenian European Union and NATO membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/April_9" title="April 9">April 9</a> – U.S. forces <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Baghdad_(2003)" title="Battle of Baghdad (2003)">seize control of Baghdad</a>, ending the <a href="/wiki/Ba%27athist_Iraq" title="Ba&#39;athist Iraq">Ba'athist regime</a> of <a href="/wiki/Saddam_Hussein" title="Saddam Hussein">Saddam Hussein</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_12" title="April 12">April 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">Hungary</a> approves joining the European Union in <a href="/wiki/2003_Hungarian_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Hungarian European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_14" title="April 14">April 14</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Human_Genome_Project" title="Human Genome Project">Human Genome Project</a> is completed, with 99% of the human <a href="/wiki/Genome" title="Genome">genome</a> sequenced to 99.99% accuracy.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_29" title="April 29">April 29</a> – The United States announces the withdrawal of its troops stationed in <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>, and the redeployment of some at the <a href="/wiki/Al_Udeid_Air_Base" title="Al Udeid Air Base">Al Udeid Air Base</a> in <a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/May_11" title="May 11">May 11</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Benvenuto_Cellini" title="Benvenuto Cellini">Benvenuto Cellini's</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Cellini_Salt_Cellar" title="Cellini Salt Cellar">Cellini Salt Cellar</a></i> table sculpture is stolen from the <a href="/wiki/Kunsthistorisches_Museum" title="Kunsthistorisches Museum">Kunsthistorisches Museum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> approves joining the European Union in <a href="/wiki/2003_Lithuanian_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Lithuanian European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_12" title="May 12">May 12</a> – In <a href="/wiki/Riyadh" title="Riyadh">Riyadh</a>, Saudi Arabia, over 30 people are killed in <a href="/wiki/Riyadh_compound_bombings" title="Riyadh compound bombings">multiple bombings at a housing compound</a>, mostly foreign expatriates.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_17" title="May 17">May 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/Slovakia" title="Slovakia">Slovakia</a> approves joining the European Union in <a href="/wiki/2003_Slovak_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Slovak European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_23" title="May 23">May 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Dewey_(deer)" title="Dewey (deer)">Dewey</a>, the first deer cloned by scientists at <a href="/wiki/Texas_A%26M_University" title="Texas A&amp;M University">Texas A&amp;M University</a>, is born.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_24" title="May 24">May 24</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Eurovision_Song_Contest_2003" title="Eurovision Song Contest 2003">Eurovision Song Contest 2003</a> takes place in <a href="/wiki/Riga" title="Riga">Riga</a>, <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a>, and is won by <a href="/wiki/Turkey_in_the_Eurovision_Song_Contest" title="Turkey in the Eurovision Song Contest">Turkish</a> entrant <a href="/wiki/Sertab_Erener" title="Sertab Erener">Sertab Erener</a> with the song "<a href="/wiki/Every_Way_That_I_Can" class="mw-redirect" title="Every Way That I Can">Every Way That I Can</a>".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_26" title="May 26">May 26</a> – <a href="/wiki/Rwanda" title="Rwanda">Rwanda</a> adopts a new constitution, which among other things, changes the country's official name from "Rwandese Republic" to "Republic of Rwanda".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_28" title="May 28">May 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Prometea" title="Prometea">Prometea</a>, the world's first cloned <a href="/wiki/Horse" title="Horse">horse</a>, is born.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/June_8" title="June 8">June 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> approves joining the European Union in <a href="/wiki/2003_Polish_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Polish European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_14" title="June 14">June 14</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a> approves joining the European Union in <a href="/wiki/2003_Czech_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Czech European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_30" title="June 30">June 30</a> – Warring parties in the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> sign a peace accord, bringing an end to the <a href="/wiki/Second_Congo_War" title="Second Congo War">Second Congo War</a>, which left millions dead.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/July_5" title="July 5">July 5</a> &#8211; Severe acute respiratory syndrome is declared to be contained by the World Health Organization.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_6" title="July 6">July 6</a> &#8211; The 70-meter Eupatoria Planetary Radar sends a <a href="/wiki/Active_SETI" title="Active SETI">METI</a> message <a href="/wiki/Cosmic_Call_2" class="mw-redirect" title="Cosmic Call 2">Cosmic Call 2</a> to five stars: Hip 4872, HD 245409, <a href="/wiki/55_Cancri" title="55 Cancri">55 Cancri</a>, <a href="/wiki/HD_10307" title="HD 10307">HD 10307</a> and <a href="/wiki/47_Ursae_Majoris" title="47 Ursae Majoris">47 Ursae Majoris</a>, that will arrive at these stars in <a href="/wiki/2036" title="2036">2036</a>, <a href="/wiki/2040" title="2040">2040</a>, May <a href="/wiki/2044" title="2044">2044</a>, September 2044 and <a href="/wiki/2049" title="2049">2049</a> respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_18" title="July 18">July 18</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Convention_on_the_Future_of_Europe" title="Convention on the Future of Europe">Convention on the Future of Europe</a> finishes its work and proposes the first European Constitution.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_24" title="July 24">July 24</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Regional_Assistance_Mission_to_Solomon_Islands" title="Regional Assistance Mission to Solomon Islands">Regional Assistance Mission to the Solomon Islands</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, begins after ethnic violence engulfs the island country.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/August_5" title="August 5">August 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/2003_Marriott_Hotel_bombing" title="2003 Marriott Hotel bombing">A car bomb explodes at the Marriott Hotel</a> in <a href="/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Jakarta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, killing 12 people and injuring 150.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_11" title="August 11">August 11</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Second_Liberian_Civil_War" title="Second Liberian Civil War">Second Liberian Civil War</a> comes to an end after President <a href="/wiki/Charles_Taylor_(Liberian_politician)" title="Charles Taylor (Liberian politician)">Charles Taylor</a> resigns and flees the country.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>NATO takes over command of the <a href="/wiki/International_Security_Assistance_Force" title="International Security Assistance Force">peacekeeping force</a> in Afghanistan, marking its first major operation outside Europe in its 54-year-history.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_14" title="August 14">August 14</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Northeast_blackout_of_2003" title="Northeast blackout of 2003">Northeast blackout of 2003</a> cuts electricity to the northeastern United States and parts of Canada.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_18" title="August 18">August 18</a> – One-year-old Zachary Turner is <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Zachary_Turner" title="Murder of Zachary Turner">murdered by his mother</a> in <a href="/wiki/Conception_Bay_South" title="Conception Bay South">Conception Bay South</a>, Canada. She had controversially been bailed and granted custody of the toddler despite facing extradition and trial for the murder of Zachary's father. The case inspired the movie <i><a href="/wiki/Dear_Zachary" class="mw-redirect" title="Dear Zachary">Dear Zachary</a></i> and prompted a change in Canadian law.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_25" title="August 25">August 25</a> – The unmanned <a href="/wiki/Spitzer_Space_Telescope" title="Spitzer Space Telescope">Spitzer Space Telescope</a> is launched from <a href="/wiki/Cape_Canaveral" title="Cape Canaveral">Cape Canaveral</a>, <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_27" title="August 27">August 27</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a> makes its <a href="/wiki/Opposition_(astronomy)" title="Opposition (astronomy)">closest approach</a> to Earth in over 60,000 years.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The first <a href="/wiki/Six-party_talks" title="Six-party talks">six-party talks</a>, involving South and North Korea, the United States, China, Japan and Russia, convene to find a peaceful resolution to the security concerns of the <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korean nuclear weapons program</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/September_4" title="September 4">September 4</a> &#8211; Europe's busiest shopping centre,<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> the <a href="/wiki/Bull_Ring,_Birmingham" title="Bull Ring, Birmingham">Bull Ring</a> in <a href="/wiki/Birmingham" title="Birmingham">Birmingham</a>, is officially opened.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_14" title="September 14">September 14</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a> approves joining the European Union in <a href="/wiki/2003_Estonian_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Estonian European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_15" title="September 15">September 15</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_(Colombia)" title="National Liberation Army (Colombia)">ELN</a> rebels kidnap eight foreign tourists at <a href="/wiki/Ciudad_Perdida" title="Ciudad Perdida">Ciudad Perdida</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>, being freed 100 days later following negotiations with the Colombian government.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_20" title="September 20">September 20</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a> approves joining the European Union in <a href="/wiki/2003_Latvian_European_Union_membership_referendum" title="2003 Latvian European Union membership referendum">a referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">September 24</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Hubble_Space_Telescope" title="Hubble Space Telescope">Hubble Space Telescope</a> starts the <a href="/wiki/Hubble_Ultra-Deep_Field" title="Hubble Ultra-Deep Field">Hubble Ultra-Deep Field</a>, making 800 exposures, until January 16, 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_27" title="September 27">September 27</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/SMART-1" title="SMART-1">SMART-1</a>, an unmanned <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">ESA</a> spaceprobe and ESA's first mission to the moon, is launched from <a href="/wiki/Kourou" title="Kourou">Kourou</a>, <a href="/wiki/French_Guiana" title="French Guiana">French Guiana</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_29" title="September 29">September 29</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Juan" title="Hurricane Juan">Hurricane Juan</a> makes <a href="/wiki/Landfall" title="Landfall">landfall</a> in <a href="/wiki/Halifax,_Nova_Scotia" title="Halifax, Nova Scotia">Halifax</a>. Causing over $265 million (2003 <a href="/wiki/CAD" class="mw-redirect" title="CAD">CAD</a>)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/October_1" title="October 1">October 1</a> – The popular and controversial English-language <a href="/wiki/Imageboard" title="Imageboard">imageboard</a> <a href="/wiki/4chan" title="4chan">4chan</a> is launched.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_5" title="October 5">October 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> warplanes <a href="/wiki/Ain_es_Saheb_airstrike" title="Ain es Saheb airstrike">strike</a> alleged Islamic jihad bases inside <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> territory, the first Israeli attack on the country since the 1973 <a href="/wiki/Yom_Kippur_War" title="Yom Kippur War">Yom Kippur War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_15" title="October 15">October 15</a> – China launches <i><a href="/wiki/Shenzhou_5" title="Shenzhou 5">Shenzhou 5</a></i>, their first <a href="/wiki/Human_spaceflight" title="Human spaceflight">manned spaceflight</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_24" title="October 24">October 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Concorde" title="Concorde">Concorde</a> makes its last commercial flight, bringing the era of airliner <a href="/wiki/Supersonic_transport" title="Supersonic transport">supersonic travel</a> to an end.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/November_12" title="November 12">November 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/2003_Nasiriyah_bombing" title="2003 Nasiriyah bombing">A suicide bombing</a> at an <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> military police headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Nasiriyah" title="Nasiriyah">Nasiriyah</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>, kills 17 Italian military police officers and nine Iraqi civilians.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_23" title="November 23">November 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/President_of_Georgia" title="President of Georgia">Georgian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Eduard_Shevardnadze" title="Eduard Shevardnadze">Eduard Shevardnadze</a> resigns after <a href="/wiki/Rose_Revolution" title="Rose Revolution">widespread protests</a> engulf the country following a disputed <a href="/wiki/2003_Georgian_parliamentary_election" title="2003 Georgian parliamentary election">parliamentary election</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_26" title="November 26">November 26</a> – The supersonic passenger jet, <a href="/wiki/Concorde" title="Concorde">Concorde</a>, makes its last ever flight from <a href="/wiki/Heathrow_Airport" title="Heathrow Airport">Heathrow Airport</a> in London to <a href="/wiki/Bristol_Filton_Airport" title="Bristol Filton Airport">Bristol Filton Airport</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/December_13" title="December 13">December 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Saddam_Hussein" title="Saddam Hussein">Saddam Hussein</a>, the former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Iraq" title="President of Iraq">president of Iraq</a>, <a href="/wiki/Operation_Red_Dawn" title="Operation Red Dawn">is captured</a> in the small town of <a href="/wiki/Ad-Dawr" title="Ad-Dawr">Ad-Dawr</a> by the U.S. Army.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">December 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Great_Socialist_People%27s_Libyan_Arab_Jamahiriya" class="mw-redirect" title="Great Socialist People&#39;s Libyan Arab Jamahiriya">Libya</a> agrees to eliminate all of its materials, equipment, and programs aimed at <a href="/wiki/Libya_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="Libya and weapons of mass destruction">producing weapons of mass destruction</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_23" title="December 23">December 23</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/World_Tourism_Organization" title="World Tourism Organization">World Tourism Organization</a> becomes a specialized agency of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/PetroChina" title="PetroChina">PetroChina</a> Chuandongbei natural gas field explosion, Guoqiao, Kai County, <a href="/wiki/Chongqing" title="Chongqing">Chongqing</a>, China, killing at least 234.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_26" title="December 26">December 26</a> – The 6.6 M<sub>w</sub>&#8239; <a href="/wiki/2003_Bam_earthquake" title="2003 Bam earthquake">Bam earthquake</a> shakes southeastern <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> with a maximum <a href="/wiki/Modified_Mercalli_intensity_scale" title="Modified Mercalli intensity scale">Mercalli intensity</a> of IX (<i>Violent</i>), killing an estimated 30,000 people.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_29" title="December 29">December 29</a> – The last known speaker of the <a href="/wiki/Akkala_S%C3%A1mi_language" title="Akkala Sámi language">Akkala Sámi language</a> dies, rendering it extinct.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February_2">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<li><a href="/wiki/October_17" title="October 17">October 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/Janice_Rule" title="Janice Rule">Janice Rule</a>, American actress (b. <a href="/wiki/1931" title="1931">1931</a>)</li>
